 is study main lagbhag saadhe teen hajaar logon ke saath baatcheet kii gai or iske rigelt kaaphi chaukaaney vaale the

 V

 nishchit rup se is prayaas ke liye sanjay badhai ke paatr hai
 The whole personality of Pandit Deendayal Upadhyaya has been assessed by dividing the book into five parts

 How Deendayal was a supporter of Akhand Bharat, how he defined cultural nationalism, what the Panditji conceptualized 'vasudhaiva Kutumbakam', commendable efforts to make the readers aware of his works and efforts for the all round development and upliftment of society
 has gone
 saanskrithik rashtrawaad ke sambandh main dow
 Mahesh Chand Sharma says that according to 'guruji' Shri Golwalkar, there are two types of nationalism
 pehla bhu-saanskrithik rashtrawaad or doosraa raajnneetik kshetreey rashtrawaad ( politico territorial nationalism )
 Geocultural nationalism is humanitarian whereas political regional nationalism is the creator of militancy and imperialism
 samskruti tatv hi rashtriyatv kaa niamak hota he
 According to Deendayal, the confluence of all flows is necessary in the virtuous stream of Bhagirathi of integrity
 yamuna bhi milegi or apni sari kalimaa khokar ganga kii dhaval dhara main ekarup ho jaaegi
 Dr
 on Deendayal's Integral Meaning Thinking
 bajranglal gupta ne vichaar rakhe hai

 tippaniyan This bridge of the country will work to connect the two northeastern states of the country, Assam and Arunachal Pradesh
 sadiya or dhola ko jodne vaale is pul ko dhola-sadiya brahmaputra pul kaa naam diya gaya he
 The importance of this bridge is not only related to the development of its people, but it will also play an important partnership strategically
 is pul ke ban jane se sudur uttar purv ke logon ke liye aane jane kii suvidha ho jaaegi, kaarobaar ko badhaava milegaa saath hi iske chaalu hone se sena ko assam ke post se arunachal-china border par pahunchane main aasaani hogi
 Let us know the characteristics of this magnificent bridge dhola-sadiya pul kii lambaai 9
 In this sense, it is 30% longer than the bandra-worli sea-link, this bridge is 540 km from Assam's capital Dispur and 300 km from Itanagar, the capital of Arunachal, aerial distance or air distance of China's border is 100 km
 After the Kalibhomora bridge near Tezpur, there is no other bridge in the middle till the next 375 km Yali Dhola on the Brahmaputra, yet all the business across the river in this area is done through boats
 Hey are ise banane kaa kaam 2011 main shuru hua or is puure project kii laagat 950 karod kii he
 The bridge rests on 182 pillars that will connect the two northeastern states of assam-arunachal, besides public transportation and business, it will also facilitate the movement of the army, it will reduce the journey to China border by 4 hours
 It has been made strong that 60 ton main battle tank can also pass, not only that it can easily withstand earthquake shock
 desh kaa yah pul desh ke do purvottar rajyon assam or arunachal pradesh ko jodne kaa kaam karegaa
 This bridge connecting Sadia and Dhola is named dhola-sadia Brahmaputra Bridge
 is pul kii ahmiyat naa sirf yahaan ke logon ke vikaas se judi he, balki samrik taur par bhi yah ahm bhagidaari nibhaayega
 The construction of this bridge will facilitate movement of people from far north east, boost business as well as its commissioning will help the army to reach the arunachal-china border from Assam post
 aaiye jaanate hai is shandaar pul kii khaasiyaten Length of dhola-sadia Bridge 9
 15 kimi he is lihaaj se yah bandra-varli si-link se bhi 30% lanbaa he yah pul assam kii rajdhani dispur se 540 kimi or arunachal kii rajdhani itanagar se 300 kimi dur he china kii seemaa kaa arial dystence yaa hawaii duuri 100 kimi se bhi kam kii he tejpur ke kareeb kalaibhomora pul ke baad brahmaputra par agle 375 kimi yaali dhola tak bich main koi doosraa pul nahin he abhi tak is ilaake main nadi ke aarpaar saare kaarobaar naavon ke jariye hi hote rahe hai
 Its construction started in 2011 and the cost of this entire project is 950 crores
 ye pul 182 khambhon par tikaa he jo purvottar ke do rajyon assam-arunachal ko jodega janata ke aane-jane or kaarobaar ke alaava, isse sena kii awajahi main bhi behad suvidha hogi isse china seemaa tak ke safar main 4 ghante kii katautee hogi pul itnaa majboot banaaya gaya he ki 60 ton ke main battle tanks bhi guzar saken itnaa hi nahin ye bukamp ke jatke bhi aasaani se jhel saktaa he
 Let us know the characteristics of this magnificent bridge dhola-sadiya pul kii lambaai 9
 In this sense, it is 30% longer than the bandra-worli sea-link, this bridge is 540 km from Assam's capital Dispur and 300 km from Itanagar, the capital of Arunachal, aerial distance or air distance of China's border is 100 km
 After the Kalibhomora bridge near Tezpur, there is no other bridge in the middle till the next 375 km Yali Dhola on the Brahmaputra, yet all the business across the river in this area is done through boats
 Hey are ise banane kaa kaam 2011 main shuru hua or is puure project kii laagat 950 karod kii he
 The bridge rests on 182 pillars that will connect the two northeastern states of assam-arunachal, besides public transportation and business, it will also facilitate the movement of the army, it will reduce the journey to China border by 4 hours
 It has been made strong that 60 ton main battle tank can also pass, not only that it can easily withstand earthquake shock
 bhartiya police main class van officer yani ki IPS banane ke liye civil sarvice exam clear karnaa hota he
 The UPSC (union Public Service Commission) conducts this exam every year
 har saal lakhon ummidavaar is exam main baithte hai, lekin sirf kuch logon kaa hi final sellection hota he
 So if you want to become an IPS, then get ready for hard work
 shaikshik yogyata or umr simabharat / nepal / bhutan ke graduate ummidavaar IPS exam main baith sakate hai
 Candidates should be between 21-30 years of age
 essi / asti shrenee ke ummidavaaron ko paanch saal kii chhot di jaati he
 Physical Qualification: Length of male candidate should be at least 165 centimeters
 160 centimetre ke SC / OBC ummidavaar bhi aplai kar sakate hai
 The length of female candidates should be 150 cm
 145 centimetre kii SC / OBC mahila ummidavaar bhi aplai kar sakati hai
 Chest: At least 84 centimeters for men
 mahilaon ke liye kam se kam 79 centimetre
 Eye site: Healthy eye vision should be 6 / 6 or 6 / 9
 kamjor ankhon kaa vijan 6 / 12 or 6 / 9 hona chahie
 Exam: For the appointment of IAS, IFS, IPS, IRS and other administrative posts, the civil service exam conducted by UPSC has to be cleared
 is exam ke do charan hote hai: prilimneri exam (prilims) or main exam
 1
 prilims exam:isamen 200-200 ankon ke do paper hote hai
 In both papers, objective type questions are asked: Paper I: This paper of 200 marks consists of National and International Current Affairs, Indian History and Indian National Movement, Geography of India and the World, Indian Monarchy and Governance (constitution , Political system, panchayati raj, public policy), economic and social development (sustainable development, poverty, population), environment Objective questions are asked from subjects such as mental ecology, bio-diversity, climate change and general science
 is paper ko atempt karne ke liye samay seemaa 2 ghante he
 Paper II: This paper of 200 marks asks questions related to comprehension, interpersonal skills, logical reasoning and analytical ability, decision making and problem solving, general mental ability, basic generality and data interpretation (charts, graphs, tables)
 is paper ko atempt karne ke liye samay seemaa 2 ghante he
 2
 main exam:civil services ke main exam main likhit pariksha or intervyuu shaamil he

 Rashtriya Janata Dal (RJD) president and former railway minister Lalu Prasad Yadav has questioned the utility of Prime Minister Narendra Modi's ambitious bullet train project
 unhone mangalvaar ko is bare main ek patr likhaa he
 Lalu has asked many questions related to the bullet train project through this letter and sought an answer from the Prime Minister
 lalu ne is patr kii ek prati rail mantri suresh prabhu ko bhi bheji he
 In the letter, Lalu has written that in the country where lakhs of people die every year due to poverty, disease and malnutrition, what is the rationale of a bullet train project costing about one lakh crore rupees? Describing the project as 'white elephant', he said that there is a need to spend so much money for just one project
 tippaniyan Lalu has further written, 'how expensive this short distance project will benefit the population of the country is an example of the mismatched priorities of the central government
 ' unhone kisaanon or garibon ke hiton kii andekhi kaa aarope lagaate hue kaha he ki ek lakh karod rupye laagat vaali is pariyojna kii jarurat ke sambandh main pradhanmantri or rail mantralay ko chahie ki ve desh ko is bare main bataaen
